Annual Report of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps Commander

1933 Was a Peaceful Year

Construction Started on the Volunteer Corps Headquarters Building

Colonel Thomas, the recently relieved Commander of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps, submitted his work report for the past year to the Municipal Council, stating that in March of that year, the various units of the Volunteer Corps were thoroughly inspected by Major General Fleming, Commander of the British Forces in Shanghai. According to his inspection report, the Corps is capable of defending the Settlement and assisting the police

in maintaining order

and security. 1933 was a peaceful year, so the Volunteer Corps was not ordered to mobilize. The Corps members were diligent in their inspection and training, and their efficiency improved daily. However, there is still a need for progress in drills such as unit transfers. As for the firearms used, the number of automatic weapons has been increasing daily. The Corps members have not slackened in their training in this area. However, the number of personnel is insufficient, far from the prescribed number. This is extremely important for the defense of the Settlement. The purpose of the B-level reserve team was to attract veterans to join, but after forming two teams, the number of applicants has been

extremely disappointing.

This must be addressed urgently. Construction has started on the Volunteer Corps headquarters building, and each team will now have a delivery room to facilitate communication. This will be convenient not only during mobilization but also on ordinary days. Furthermore, a manager has been assigned to the shooting range, which has been needed for a long time, greatly benefiting the training of Corps members. The Russian unit has achieved excellent results as before after the commander was assigned. Most of the unit members have been replaced by young people, who are comparable to the old members, and they pay close attention to exercise. The Corps members are healthy and satisfactory. Colonel Thomas expressed his deep gratitude to the Board of Directors for their support and to the various departments of the Municipal Council for their

cooperative spirit.

He was especially proud of the Corps members' service and spirit of sacrifice. Regarding the number of Corps members, the prescribed number for the Chinese unit in the Volunteer Corps is five

officers and 120 members. The current number is seven officers and 164 members, including active duty and A-level reservists, which exceeds the prescribed number.

Guangdong Association Pays Attention to the Case of Six Westerners Raping a Chinese Woman

After Guangdong woman Wang Zhang was gang-raped and robbed by six Westerners, the Guangdong Association in Shanghai, upon hearing the news, immediately sent personnel to investigate the circumstances of the rape and robbery at 5 Renzhi Lane, in order to file a lawsuit in the future. The Association also designated Association Supervisor Guo Qiming, a lawyer, as a pro bono lawyer to handle the case, and sent letters to all sectors for assistance in order to maintain security and suppress the strong and domineering.

Grand Opening of the Radio Station Staff Association Meeting

The Shanghai Radio Station of the Ministry of Transportation, in order to promote unity and develop the business, established a staff association organization in January of last year. After one year of operation, the association, in accordance with its bylaws, held a general membership meeting yesterday at the Guyixuan Restaurant on Sanma Road. Over 200 members attended, creating a lively and joyful atmosphere. The meeting officially began at 6:00 PM. Association Secretary Wang Zhengwei and Accountant Xie Chunpu reported on the work done over the past year, followed by a discussion of several important proposals. After the meeting, a dinner was held, and various businesses in the city donated valuable items, which the association numbered and distributed to the members through a lottery to provide entertainment. During the dinner, Lu Guixiang also gave a speech. The event ended with great joy at around 10:00 PM.

News from the Jing'an Temple Office of the Bank of China

The Jing'an Temple Office of the Bank of China, located at the intersection of Yu Garden Road, has been open for twenty days, and its deposit and remittance business has been very successful. Because the bank has branches everywhere and the remittance fees are low, and no remittance fees are charged for small amounts, the total amount remitted has been quite considerable. In order to facilitate customers, the office also acts as an agent for all trust deposits of the head office's trust department and all foreign exchange matters of the international department. All types of fixed deposit accounts for children's education, marriage, old-age care, public welfare organizations, fixed deposit accounts, and trust deposits can be opened at this office. Foreign currency trading can also be arranged directly with this office.

Pudong Eggs Accumulate in Large Quantities; International Trade Bureau Plans to Promote Use

Letter from Chuansha County Government Seeks Solutions

The County Produces Over Three Million Eggs Annually

Pudong has long been famous for its egg production, so farmers generally regard raising chickens as an important side business. The eggs produced are sold in this city. However, due to the economic downturn and commercial stagnation in recent years, sales have been greatly affected, resulting in large-scale accumulation in rural areas. In light of this, the Chuansha County Government has sent a special letter to the International Trade Bureau in this port, requesting assistance in finding outlets and developing sales plans. The original letter roughly stated: This county has 26,557 households, each of which usually raises Pudong laying hens. On average, each household produces 120 eggs per year, totaling 3,864,840 eggs annually. Recently, due to stagnant sales, households' interest in raising chickens has waned, which has also affected the county's chicken-raising promotion plan. The only solution now is to find ways to expand egg sales. We kindly request you to investigate and determine export outlets for this trade, so that farmers' livelihoods can be improved, and so on. After receiving the letter, the International Trade Bureau immediately instructed the Guidance Department to draft a plan and reply.

Municipal Police Bureau Earnestly Requests Allocation of Winter Clothing

Letter to Xinwei Relief Association

The Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau sent a letter yesterday to the Xinwei Relief Association, requesting the allocation of thirty sets each of men's and women's winter clothing for relief purposes. The original letter stated: The Bureau handles an increasing number of relief cases daily, including suicide attempts by drowning and cases of abducted women and children, many of whom are scantily clad and unable to withstand the cold, making them vulnerable to freezing to death. Previously, winter clothing donated by various charitable organizations has been distributed as needed and is now exhausted. Knowing of your association's enthusiastic charitable efforts and unwavering commitment, we specifically request you to promptly allocate thirty sets each of men's and women's winter clothing for relief purposes to complete this good deed. We also hope to receive a reply.

Achievements of the Shanghai Mental Hospital

Recently Cured and Discharged: Sang Housheng and Jiang Zicheng

It is already unbearably painful for the poor and sick in the world, but it is even more painful for those suffering from mental illness. Since Mr. Gu Wenjun of Chuansha founded the Shanghai Mental Hospital on Guling Road, Ren'an Lane, it has cured more than a hundred men and women with mental illnesses. It is reported that recently, Sang Housheng and Jiang Zicheng were cured and discharged from the hospital. They were initially severely mentally ill, but after being sent to the hospital for treatment by their families, they were both cured and discharged in less than a month.

Manager and Apprentice Die from Coal Gas Poisoning

At No. 34 Rongchang Lane, Dongyouheng Road, Hongkou, Xu Zengfu (age 22, from Nanjing), the manager of the Yicheng Yarn Belt Factory, and his apprentice Zhang Xincai (age 17), along with friends Fan Kaiyou and Ni Baochun, slept in the same room. Yesterday, due to the severe cold, they closed the doors and windows tightly and placed a coal briquette stove in the room for heating. Unexpectedly, after the four fell asleep, the small room was filled with fumes all night, and all of them suffered from coal gas poisoning. When colleagues broke into the room around 7 a.m. the next morning, they saw Xu and the others lying unconscious on the bed. Realizing that they had been poisoned, they rushed them to Tongren Hospital for treatment. After the doctors administered injections and medication, Fan and Ni were fortunate enough to recover, but Xu Zengfu and Zhang Xincai died one after another due to excessive poisoning. The bodies were then transported by special vehicle to the coroner's office, pending examination by the court this morning.

Dancer Sues for Seduction and Abandonment

Luo Meimei, a dancer from Ningbo at the Vienna Dance Hall, recently hired lawyer Zhou Yongding to file a lawsuit with the Criminal Court of the First Special District Court, accusing Zou Shunsun, a local resident and owner of the China Woodware Company at No. 660 Jing'an Temple Road, of seducing her into illicit relations and abandoning her. She requested that he be punished according to the law and, in a separate civil suit, demanded a one-time payment of 11,440 yuan for living expenses. Her complaint has already been published in the newspaper. Yesterday afternoon was the scheduled date for the trial, but the defendant, Zou Shunsun, did not appear. Lawyer Gu Hanli appeared in court on his behalf and requested a postponement, stating that Zou was currently collecting accounts in Nanjing. The plaintiff, Luo Meimei, appeared with her lawyer, Zhou. Judge Xue Lanru questioned Luo Meimei about her age and place of origin. Because the defendant was absent, the case could not proceed, and the hearing was postponed to the afternoon of the 30th of this month.

Apprentice's Tragic Death Case Postponed Pending Examination by the Municipal Council

Shi Shaoxing, an apprentice at the Xufutai Western Tailor Shop on Dalian Bay Road, died suddenly. When the authorities examined the body, a hole was found in the back of his head, with blood flowing freely. The forensic doctor determined that the injury was caused by a sharp pair of scissors before death. However, the shop owner, Xu Futai, and his wife, Ms. Chen, both denied committing the crime, while the deceased's uncle, Shi Qixiang, insisted that he had been brutally murdered by the Xu couple. Lawyer Wu Peng filed a criminal lawsuit against Xu and his wife for cruel murder, requesting the death penalty. This has been reported in this newspaper. The case was heard yesterday afternoon by Judge Wu Zehan of the First Special District Court. The defendants, Xu Futai and his wife, failed to appear despite being summoned. The plaintiff, Shi Qixiang, testified that the deceased was his second nephew. On the night of the 13th of this month, his eldest nephew, Shaozhou, came to report that Shaoxing had died. However, on the night of the 12th, the two brothers had come to his place to borrow money to return to their hometown. On the morning of the 13th, Shaozhou saw him drinking water on the road and borrowed money from Shaozhou to buy snacks. On the morning of the 15th, he went to the coroner's office and suddenly saw blood flowing from the right side of the deceased's head, and his clothes were stained with blood. The blood on the cement floor was also not yet dry. The deceased had often told him that the shop owner and his wife treated him very harshly and often beat him. Therefore, this tragic death must have been a case of murder, and he demanded a strict investigation, and so on. Shi Shaozhou then took the stand and testified that he saw Shaoxing drinking water on the road on the morning of the 13th and gave him money to buy snacks, after which he did not see him again. The deceased had no previous illness, and his mind was normal. At 5 p.m. on the 13th, he suddenly heard the old clerk say that his brother had died. He rushed to Xu Futai's shop and saw his brother's body, which was already stiff, and saw blood near his head, especially a lot of blood at the back of his head, a tragic sight to behold. He immediately rushed to inform his uncle and accompanied him to the coroner's office on the morning of the 15th, and so on. The court had previously instructed the Health Department of the Municipal Council to examine the cause of the injury to the deceased's head, but no report has yet been received. The hearing was adjourned to a later date.

Coal Gas Poisoning Nearly Claims Three Lives

Chen Liansheng, a Ningbo native living at No. 18 Luoxiang Local House, Hudong District, works in a Yangshupu yarn factory. His hard-earned income is sufficient for food and clothing. His wife, Sun, 25 years old, was due to give birth, and suddenly went into labor a few days ago. He hired a midwife, Ms. He, to assist with the delivery, and also lit a charcoal stove for warmth. Unexpectedly, the house was small and narrow, without doors and windows. Chen Liansheng's sister, Zhu Yuan, entered the room after shopping and saw her sister-in-law lying stiffly on the bed, while the midwife had fainted on the floor, and the baby was also breathless. She then felt the coal gas fumes, which were unbearable. She cried for help loudly. Neighbors gathered, and opinions varied, but no one knew what to do. Fortunately, a neighboring woman was quick-witted and sent someone to inform Liansheng and also called female doctors Qian Shuzhen, Yuan Huiyu, and Xu Cuizhen of the Hongkou People's Maternity Hospital to rush to the rescue. They said it was caused by coal gas poisoning. At that time, the parturient's uterus had also prolapsed, so surgery was performed to restore it to its original position. Fortunately, the poisoning was mild, and the parturient and midwife regained consciousness one after another. The baby was cyanotic all over, and although artificial respiration was used to barely save it, it was in a terrible state.

Fire at the Intersection of Xujiahui Road and Luban Road in the French Concession This Morning

At approximately 1:10 a.m. this morning, a fire broke out at No. 275, at the intersection of Xujiahui Road and Luban Road in the French Concession. The flames immediately broke through the roof and were extremely fierce. The fire brigade rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire. As of the time this newspaper went to press, it had not yet been extinguished. The exact amount of the loss is unknown.

Minutes of the Meeting of the Fifth Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Association

According to Guowen News Agency, the Fifth District Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Association held its fifteenth executive committee meeting at 8:00 p.m. yesterday. More than ten committee members attended, including He Yuanming, Fang Boqin, Feng Song, Gong Jingyan, Hu Zifang, Xu Zixian, Zhang Huichang, Wu Yunlu, and others. Qu Zhenhua presided over the meeting. Matters discussed: (1) Regarding the letter from the Liyuanfang Branch requesting rent reduction, it was resolved to forward it to the general association for review. (2) Regarding the investigation of dog racing tracks and Jai Alai in the French Concession, which are related to gambling and harmful to citizens, it was resolved to request the general association and the ratepayers' association to negotiate with the French authorities to ban them. (3) Regarding the date of the second members' congress of this association, it was resolved to hold it at 2:00 p.m. on February 25. (4) Regarding the request to amend the provisions of the civil code's lease regulations to benefit citizens, it was resolved to send letters to the general association and the First Special District Citizens' Association to jointly advocate for it. (5) Regarding the investigation of plainclothes detectives from the French patrol room who wear no badges when performing their duties, which can easily lead to misunderstandings, it was resolved to request the authorities to add special marks in the future to prevent criminals from impersonating them, to ensure public safety. It was resolved to send a letter to the Chinese ratepayers' association of the French Concession to negotiate with the French authorities. The meeting adjourned after the discussions were completed.

Recent News from Tongchang Vacuum Flask Factory. The Tongchang Vacuum Flask Factory in Jiumu, Shanghai, is one of the earliest and most widely distributed vacuum flask manufacturers in this port. Its Tongxing brand vacuum flasks pay special attention to the flask core in manufacturing, and the air is completely extracted, which is not only durable but also keeps warm and cold for a longer time. Moreover, the factory's equipment focuses on practicality, the cost is lower, and the price is also cheaper. Therefore, it sells well in the Yangtze River basin and the Minyue Nanyang area and can compete with foreign goods. Recently, the factory, in view of the easy rusting of the bottom of the flasks, has started using white copper for the bottom of the newly released three-pound and four-pound painted and new-pattern vacuum flasks. Although the cost is higher, one bottle with a white copper bottom can be used as long as two bottles with ordinary galvanized iron bottoms. The factory has now specially made the latest military vacuum flasks, which are suitable for Boy Scouts, business guard groups, and students, and are very convenient to carry when traveling.

Publishing World

Recent News from the Medical Review Monthly. The Medical Review Monthly was founded by Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, and edited by Song Guobin, Standing Chairman of the National Physicians' Association. The writers are all leading figures in the medical field. The first issue of the sixth volume was published on time on the 15th.

In addition to more than 20 articles commenting on Chinese and Western medicine, this issue contains the original manuscript of President Wang Jingwei's speech welcoming the Third National Physicians' Annual Meeting, which is thousands of words long, insightful, and worthy of being called a famous theory. Since its publication, the publication has never increased its price. Twelve issues per year, including postage, cost one yuan domestically and two yuan and fifty cents abroad. Sample copies are sent with a one-cent postage stamp. There are currently more than 8,000 subscribers at home and abroad. It is distributed by the Medical Review Society, No. 408 Albert Road, Shanghai.

The Bestselling of "Respecting Confucius and Notes on Confucianism." The collection of "Respecting Confucius in Past Dynasties and Foreign Notes on Confucianism," compiled by Cheng Baijia and published by the China Moral Society, has been reprinted seven times in eight months, with a total of more than 10,000 copies printed. The content includes the records of respecting Confucius in the past dynasties and the theories of scholars from Europe and the United States on Confucianism, such as Weixi Qin, Li Jiabai (USA), Li Timotai (UK), Yishaling (Russia), Duomas (France), Feixili (Germany), Nadun (Italy), Youhe Changxiong (Japan), and others, more than 30 articles, more than 20 illustrations, and more than 100,000 words. Wang Yiting, Wang Qingmu, Kong Xiangxi, Dai Chuanxian, Li Yunshu, Chen Qicai, Gao Chuiwan, Zhu Qinglan, Wu Peifu, each printed 1,000 to 300 copies, and distributed them to relatives and friends.

Reading Problems

How to Train Our Minds (2)

Reply to Mr. Xu Lezhen (continued)

In short: Our attitude toward a person's pursuit of knowledge should be:

(1) For the practical use of life, starting from needs, and strongly denying the attitude of "learning for the sake of learning";

(2) Learning life from life, reading is just a means; cultivating the organization of our minds from life, not relying solely on a certain rationality.

(3) Not creating a perfect person first and then recognizing society, but gradually expanding the boundaries of recognition in the struggle of social life; recognizing the reality of the environment is our most urgent need; but we do not

Can we look at it coldly and be satisfied? What should we do after we know it? We still have to do something!

The above is a superficial contribution to your attitude. Whether it is correct, I hope you and the general readers will correct it. Below, I will answer a few of the questions you asked: (1) The science that can train a person's mind to be rigorous, sound, and sensitive, I think the most appropriate answer is logic, but other sciences such as mathematics and natural sciences also have this effect.

(2) Logic can not only "organize our thoughts" but also correct the misconceptions of common sense. A person who does not understand logic is often trapped in contradictory thinking throughout his life, unable to correctly understand all phenomena. He often mistakenly regards fragments as the whole, showing the ignorance of "fetishism," and he is still complacent, thinking that he has grasped the truth. Therefore, some people call logic the science of methodology. It suggests the correct method of "recognition."

Studying logic does not necessarily require advanced mathematics, but it cannot be separated from "reality." It must be grasped in daily life. A person who has not attended school can also have a very logical mind. It can be seen that there is a certain logic in life, which has already implied everything to those who are loyal to life. This science can only obtain some rules in books; and it is strangely difficult to understand, but a person who has experienced life will naturally understand it as soon as he reads it.

(3) We should study materialist dialectics. But we must also read books on formal logic.

(4) The purpose of reading foreign languages ​​is a means of seeking knowledge or a need for a career. Since you have already self-studied to the ability to read foreign classics, you do not have to give up English in order to study other sciences. You better read some related English works while doing a certain study.

Finally, I still hope that you can propose a more practical and systematic personal reading plan for discussion.

Spring and Autumn

Taking Advantage of Weaknesses

— Tian Xiu

Weakness is a person's shortcoming. Whether it is a habitual habit or something done, as long as you show it significantly, you never want to cover it up, but those who are clever discover it, and like magicians, they use it in a set, and it can be taken endlessly and used inexhaustibly. On a small scale, it is a personal way to make money. If applied internationally, it is the only magic weapon for aggression! How can it be said that it is a personal way to make money? Not to mention anything else, take Shanghai as an example. It is said that there are many people who pretend to be Mu Lao (another name for Pak-to-tings), who are strong and loud in their words, and their appearance is the most popular (to be popular is to be good). They also have many errand runners who run for him and listen for him. As long as they encounter opium, gambling, red pills, strips (women), and other illegal and prohibited things, they will try their best to run into that place. Their momentum is fierce and they will first give you a threat. If you buy his account (naturally you have to buy his account), he will immediately change his tone and say that everyone is from the same family, it doesn't matter, it doesn't matter, so the big things will turn into nothing in a while, but the five or ten yuan bills have been put into their coat pockets.

Looking at culture and art, which magazines, novels, books, dramas, movies, etc. are not using this set of tricks? What they use is nothing more than the two most obvious and common points of sexual desire and superstition. Just pay attention to the advertisements in the daily newspapers to prove it. Look at the dramas performed on the stage, most of which are superstitious about theocracy and vigorously maintain the so-called cause and effect retribution. The films on the screen are marked with legs that are fragrant and no stars that are not naked, with tempting advertisements, plus a ban on selling tickets to children under the age of sixteen to attract general erotic audiences. Novels and books are also depicting the affairs of men and women, and even the social news of the daily newspapers, as long as it involves private affairs between men and women, they are vigorously publicized with great fanfare, so their publications are increasing in sales day by day. As for the use between groups, there is no need to seek far, just look at the bad neighbor who makes goodwill a cliché. At first, they took advantage of the Qing government's confusion, and in the Jiawu year, they cut off Korea and Taiwan. In the Republic of China, they took advantage of Yuan Lao Tou's desire to be emperor and signed the Twenty-One Demands. They also used the new and old warlords to seize power and provided them with weapons, ammunition, and money to fuel the civil war. Using the strategy of defeating them one by one, they easily obtained the four eastern provinces, and also used... used... The past cannot be said, and the future cannot be said, alas! I don't know if our weaknesses are too many? Or is it that people are good at using them? I need to ask the smart readers.

Anecdotes of Yao Zirang

— Qing Qu

Yao Zirang has already passed away, and the people of Shanghai mourn him. During his life, he enjoyed a reputation for integrity. Without dwelling on it, I would like to collect a few anecdotes, some of which may be unknown to people, and briefly describe them as follows:

The establishment of academies in Shanghai was first promoted by Longmen, and during the thirteenth year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty, there was the Gezhi Academy. It was established by Tang Jingxing, an observer, along with Danish lawyer Dan Wen, and Westerner Fu Lanya. They hired Tiannan Dun Sou (Wang Tao) as the supervisor of the academy, dividing the year into four seasons for setting topics and inviting the authorities to set questions for the scholars. Their merits were judged to determine the rankings, and those at the top were given rewards from the academy's funds. The authorities also allocated funds and encouraged them to boost interest. Therefore, Gezhi and Longmen were opposed. At that time, Longmen emphasized classical texts, while Gezhi focused on current affairs. Those listed in Longmen were considered the old school, while those listed in Gezhi were considered the new school.

The new school included figures such as "Wang Zuo Cai," "Zhong Tianwei," "Yin Zhi Lu," and "Xu Ke Quan," who were often ranked as super-class; while in the old school, Li Zhongjue (Ping Shu) and Yao Zirang occasionally stood out, holding the highest reputation in Longmen.

In a certain year, the education supervisor of Songjiang Prefecture, when observing local customs, set the topic as "Strategies for Coastal and Maritime Defense." Yao and Li competed. Yao argued that "preventing foreign aggression is the key to controlling the powers, and self-strengthening is the fundamental task, ultimately aiming for a situation where the emperor is virtuous and the defense lies in appeasing the barbarians," as the goal. Li, on the other hand, emphasized "the importance of the southeast sea ports, especially Wusong," with the most insightful statement being, "allowing the enemy to attack our fixed fortifications with mobile artillery, while we counter with fixed artillery against mobile ships." Yao and Li's essays were both highly praised by their teachers and included in the "Jiangzuo School Scholar Records." Yao's nephew, Liang (named Wen Dong), had a different personality from Zirang, being more rigid and conservative. He once corresponded with Tiannan Dun Sou. His younger brother sometimes mocked him, but the older brother retorted, criticizing his impracticality. Yao Zirang's son, Mengsao, unfortunately died tragically in Harbin. Upon hearing the news, everyone mourned, but his father said: "This is probably fate. I knew this would happen, but I didn't listen and it ended up like this. What else can I blame?" as if he had foreseen it. The scholarly atmosphere in Shanghai has gradually declined in recent years, and some are even criticized for academic cliques. However, Yao Zirang, amidst the ups and downs, still took it upon himself to promote integrity and eliminate corruption. Looking to the future, in the Chun Shen and Hu Du regions of Shanghai, I fear there will be no such central figure. Alas!

Spectator's Guide for Movie Theaters

— Hu Xuguang

(1) The later you arrive, the better. Movie theater patrons mostly like to stand up and let you rub past them, stepping on their toes, which they especially welcome.

(2) Before sitting down, stand and take off your coat. If the glasses of an old gentleman in the next seat or the hat of a young lady in the front row unfortunately block your coat's path, then the glasses and hat are not sensible and should go to the floor; it's none of your business. While taking off your coat, feel free to stand there for a while. The people behind you are here specifically to admire your back.

(3) Sitting on an old lady after finding the wrong seat is also something that should happen in the dark. Who told that old lady to sit according to the seat number?

(4) The synopsis must be read aloud. If you brought a girlfriend, you should explain the plot and dialogue in the film clearly, like a teacher lecturing her. The beneficiary will definitely not be just your girlfriend.

(5) When the main character in the film sings, you should clap to the rhythm and raise your voice to sing along with him. Patrons pay money, and a small part of it is to watch the play, but the majority is to listen to you sing.

(6) Predict the plot of the movie, pull on the person in the next seat, and tell them what's going to happen. Most movie theater customers are idiots, and the people sitting next to you are especially foolish. They paid money to not only watch the play but also to have their minds enlightened. Their gratitude will be endless, of course.

(7) The play should be realistic and have interruptions. You should cough a few times and spit a few times along with the plot of the movie to show realism. Sunflower seeds, peanut shells, and banana peels are also necessary interruptions.

Inside the Hongmiao Temple, incense smoke flickers. I, a devoted patriot, feel at ease in my old age.

In front of the racecourse, I feel a sense of desolation. Buildings like Hua An stand tall like black gallows in the shadows. In the night wind, the nearby street trees stretch out iron branches, clasping the silver string moon, singing naturally.

The door of Carso is half-open, flowing with hot "jazz." Eupetic rhythm involuntarily crossed inside. My stomach is already full, let's have a cup of "Kafei." Across from me is a modern girl, talking about sand crabs, but she herself is an old crab. The bright white fox collar can't hide the wrinkles at her temples.

"My wandering soul is accustomed to freedom, again treading willow catkins across Xie Bridge"... A long afterimage accompanies me on my way home.

The Night Before

— Cai Dezhi

The neon lights, inlaid in the lead-gray sky, truly resemble a dim ancient bronze mirror, a touch of red, a moment of melancholy.

All day long, cramming for the night school exam, Saturday night is a rare treat. I left the office and lightly stepped into the Le Xiang Hotel, ate a comfortable dinner. Coming outside, I felt happy in my heart, the taste of the dishes was not bad.

Passing the Palaoe Hotel, through the glass windows facing the street, gentlemen and ladies were still sipping tea leisurely. Elegant lighting, classical wall decorations, and a pianist on the music stage were playing a tune. An artistically styled hairstyle, a young man's face.

Advertisements for airline tickets, with blue backgrounds and white letters, fluttered everywhere like bargain flags. Roosevelt, the monster who advises the public to restrain their luck-seeking mentality during national crises, should first show his face on Nanjing Road, so he won't embarrass himself again next time.

Chen Yumei's hypnotic songs have already been sung all over Nanjing Road, but they are still a hit. There are so many pedestrians, and so many women. Carelessly, I bumped into someone. "Why don't you have eyes?" I only blame myself for being so engrossed in watching, earning myself a scolding for my trouble.

If there are only rough materials and unfinished products around the Great World, then this is where the refined products are. Eel-like bodies, dazzlingly decorated with poisonous scales. Charming amber, evenly spread on Claire La Belle-style powder. De Ge Paila's darling lady, a consumer of 1.4 million Western cosmetics!

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 23: Difficult to Endure the Pain, Focusing on the Music to Encourage Sentiment, Unsuccessful Farewell to the Flying Talisman

The shop assistant did not reply but smiled as he looked at him. Then he said, "Doesn't the Second Master contribute a share?" Ji Zhi said, "They didn't send me an invitation, how can I give a gift?" As he spoke, he turned around and walked towards the study in his house. His books had all been moved to the Dagongmen Village School. This was his elder brother's study. He casually took a book from the bookshelf and sat down at the writing desk to read. Opening the book, it turned out to be a copy of the Amitabha Sutra. He thought to himself, "Things in the world are so contradictory. My elder brother is a most enthusiastic person, yet he has this kind of Buddhist book on his bookshelf." So he casually opened the book and looked at the first line: "Thus have I heard: At one time, the Buddha was in the Jeta Grove, Anathapindika's Park, in the country of Shravasti." After reading it, he could guess the general meaning but could not fully understand it. Holding the book in his hand, he raised his head slightly and thought for a moment. Then he thought, "Who cares if I understand it or not, I'll just use it to relieve boredom. Fortunately, there are explanations after the sutra text, so I can patiently read on and calm myself down. Otherwise, I would go crazy today." So he carefully read the explanations and understood them clearly, then continued reading down a few lines. He felt he could barely understand a little, then came a long string of Sanskrit transliterated names of people, such as Elder Shariputra, Maha Maudgalyayana, Maha Kasyapa, Maha Katyayana... He saw that there were two lines of this, not only not knowing what they meant, but also feeling a little dizzy. Just as he was spacing out, the sound of loud music entered his ears. He thought, "This must be a flower carriage going to pick up the bride." I don't want to listen to this kind of sound, I'll go play in the backyard. At this time, his elder brother, Houzhi, had recovered from his illness by eighty or ninety percent. He placed a rattan chair in the sun in the backyard, lay on the rattan chair, and held a magazine to read. His sister-in-law was also knitting a woolen sweater on a small chair next to him. Ji Zhi slowly walked over and said to Houzhi, "You've only just recovered a little, you don't need to read." Houzhi said, "It's good you're here. After today, you can go back to school to teach tomorrow. I've already recovered, so I don't need you to take care of me at home."

(230)

Wanderings

Solitary Lament for a Cold Soul

— Feng Zi

Walking alone with a stick, not with much enthusiasm to appreciate the scenery of West Lake after a long absence. But, occasionally seeing fallen leaves on the dike and withered trees at the foot of the mountain, when a sense of winter's desolation fills my heart, a desolate heart will recognize the true meaning of life. Perhaps it's because I don't have this kind of mood when I casually invite two or three friends to hang out! Wine, women, and boring small talk will give us boundless joy. Not to mention this desolate winter afternoon, even the fragrance of flowers and songs of birds in spring would let the charming delicate voices and dazzling calves occupy the poet's spirit first. Nature doesn't want boring tourists to disturb its poetic realm. Loneliness is the return of all things. People with lonely hearts, stumbling in nature's realm of solitude, everything is silent in the silence where there is no noise. A heart like stagnant water will also ripple with the spring of life.

Frozen clouds like gray ice lie motionless, staying at home, and worrying about a furnace of red charcoal. Endless troubles are smoked by the flames until I can't breathe. "Let's take a walk outside!"

"Where to go? I guess the cold plum blossoms on Gushan have already announced the spring news!" Carrying a cane, I have decided where to go.

The bustling streets stir the beating of life. Even in the cold winter, the east end of the street is red-eyed at the automobile's power, lying in the alley and daydreaming. Let this old man eat some dim sum! After a single negotiation, he agreed to his request. A snail-like posture, regretting that I called him to pull the cart, the conflicting consciousness of selfishness and charity is stirring again.

The desolate lakeside is filled with sparse yellow leaves. White water and gray mountains, West Lake has lost its former beauty.

In winter, on a hazy, snowy winter afternoon, walking alone on Bai Causeway, I often think of the life of the poet-monk Manshu wearing a bamboo hat and straw sandals, and feel sympathy as if I experienced it myself. Ah! Manshu's life is autumn and winter.

No one on the long causeway, slowly chanting wildly, a few gusts of cold wind pass through the drooping willows, chilling people to the bone. This is a gift in loneliness, you won't meet it if you don't go out.

From the Gushan Road lined with willow branches, one can hear the roaring of steam whistles from the opposite bank, which are the shuttle buses of the Grand Auditorium Cinema. Entertaining oneself in the dark in the cinema during the day is a proper pastime for civilized people.

"If you want to ask about the news of the plum blossoms, why wait for the cranes to return!" Since Lin Hejing left the world, his loving wife and beloved children were also unwilling to stay here. It's good, the soulmate of life and death is gone, why bother staying alone and suffering unnecessary torture. The three hundred cold blossoms have long gone with the flying cranes, leaving only a few plants that are greedy for the world, which are also withered with sparse branches and flowers.

Light green, faint red, lush, delicate, the delicate makeup of the past, the lingering dream shadows, still vaguely in a piece of cold cloud, longing for past joys.

In tranquility, in coldness, I seem to hear the towering ancient trees, rustling to express some sympathy to people. Perhaps there is no such sympathy in the fickle human world!

"The plum blossoms in Gushan are not good, Lingfeng is much better, and there are more people there!"

A few exclamations floated in my ear, on the noisy way home in the car.

Education News Abroad

Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China Holds Public Exhibition in Beijing

Opening on the 28th of this month at the Institute on Chengxian Street

Ten Years of Effort Accumulating Extremely Rich Resources Domestically Unparalleled

Collecting All Species of Flounder in the World Particularly Valuable

Separate Room Dedicated to Displaying Animals and Plants Needed by Middle Schools

The Hainan Biological Science Collection Group, initiated by the Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China, departed from Beijing on the 15th of this month to collect specimens in Hainan. The staff at the Institute, feeling the recent attention of the public to biological science, and also due to the invitation of the Nanjing Middle School Teachers' Biological Research Association for the Institute to hold a public exhibition as soon as possible, so that Nanjing students and the general public can observe and learn, in order to enhance their knowledge of biological science, began to prepare for the public exhibition immediately after the departure of the Hainan Collection Group. Now everything is ready, and it is scheduled to be held in Beijing for two weeks starting on the 28th of this month. During this exhibition period, it is free to visit without purchasing tickets. The details are as follows:

Opening in Beijing for a Two-Week Period

Nanjing Biological Research Institute of the Science Society of China

, Public Exhibition, decided to open at the Institute in Wende Lane, Chengxian Street, on the 28th of this month. The exhibition period is two weeks. The exhibits this time are the research achievements of the Institute over the years. All domestic animal and plant species, regardless of high or low level, that have been studied by the Institute, are displayed one by one, labeled with scientific names, Chinese names, and place of origin, and have maps recording their distribution. It is a real-life portrayal of the native products of the country. Examining material evidence, unlike other exhibitions that emphasize ornate decoration, can be achieved in a short period of time.

Exhibits Mostly Practical Science

According to the person in charge of the Science Society of China, this time the exhibits in each room are not only pure science, materials related to taxonomy and geographical distribution, but also related to practical science. For example, the wood specimens in the plant section, the branches, leaves, fruits, seeds, and wood of each plant, and their distribution are all clearly explained one by one. Specimens and enlarged color pictures of commonly seen and edible algae are displayed. And the fungi related to agricultural crops and forest tree diseases are arranged according to the natural environment to show their natural growth state. In the animal section, such as human parasites, not only are the male and female adults collected, but also their cocoons and larvae, and even their intermediate hosts, such as snails and water snails, are collected as much as possible, and supplemented with drawings to show their life process and the symptoms of the patients. Therefore, it not only demonstrates the richness of our country's natural products and the achievements of academic research, but also shows the public's common sense of hygiene and touches on economic appreciation and use.

Valuable Varieties in the Classification Room

As for the classification room, there are many rare and valuable specimens. The cones of various pine and fir plants are displayed in taxonomic order, which is rare in the country. The specimens of the Cashew family of higher plants are particularly complete. Corals and sea lilies are displayed, and what is particularly rare is that the Institute has collected all species of flounder in the world, which are also displayed in the exhibition room, showing the panorama of flounder, which is truly a treasure trove unparalleled in the world. The collection of fish can be said to be the first in the country, and the number of other animal and plant species displayed is also difficult to compare with domestically. The Institute's ten years of effort can be seen here.

A Separate Room for Middle School Specimens

In order to meet the requirements of the Nanjing Middle School Teachers' Biological Research Association, the Institute has set up a separate room dedicated to displaying animal and plant specimens needed by middle schools, and the process of specimen taxidermy and slide preparation is also shown in detail with brief explanations, so that students can understand it at a glance. At the same time, the Institute's research papers are also stored in multiple copies in the library for sale.

Opening Ceremony

The opening ceremony was held at 9:00 am, chaired by Liu Tingfang, recorded by Yang Bingxun, and emceed by Wu Yunrui. After performing the ceremony, the chairman delivered the opening speech, briefly stating that the Chinese Educational Society was established during the national crisis. At this time of national crisis, everyone knows that education to save the country is like a distant water that cannot put out a nearby fire. However, as long as those engaged in education can make up their minds, the so-called speed is sometimes possible, and the goal can always be achieved. Therefore, although people in the education field know that educational undertakings are slow, there is nothing more important than this. Everyone must have this hope in mind, and education is the entire science of life. To save the country, we must start with education. After the establishment of this association, not much work has been done in the past. The work that should be done after this second annual meeting will be discussed at the meeting. This session is held in Beijing, and I am very grateful to the preparatory personnel in the capital and the Zhongda Luo Principal and Dean of the College of Education for their efforts and equipment, etc. Then Zhang Zifan of the Central Party Department delivered an encouraging speech, briefly stating that China has many problems to solve, but the most important is education. In the past two years, the domestic education community has published many education reform plans, and the Central Committee also resolved many proposals on education at the Third Plenary Session. But all of you can see that there are many places such as education administration, education system, education equipment, etc., that feel dissatisfied. If you want to reform many dissatisfactions, you must take care of the country and the nation. But under this modern dark society, the will of the general youth is not firm, their thoughts are troubled, some are content to degenerate, some are seeking resistance, some only know how to study, regardless of the country, and even participate in meaningless struggles. Therefore, this situation is truly an obstacle to the future of the reform movement. Therefore, on the one hand, the government is still overcoming difficulties and continuing to carry out reforms, and on the other hand, it hopes that the education community will lead the youth, correct their mistakes, and carry out reforms on the same track. The Chinese Educational Society is organized by well-known people in the education field. In the future, it will study good methods and plans to help the government and guide the youth. The future is very promising, etc. Then Gu Shusen of the Ministry of Education delivered an encouraging speech, briefly stating that he is a member, although Minister Wang ordered him to represent the meeting, but speaking as a member, since the outbreak of the national crisis in China, the education administration has paid special attention to national rejuvenation and production education. Therefore, in recent years, the Ministry of Education has made changes to the curriculum and revisions to laws and regulations based on these two major goals. However, the regulations drafted by the Ministry are mostly subjective and have too few objective opinions. Because the domestic education community itself does not have the organization of academic research groups, the opinions sought are only sought from those known by private individuals, which is not as effective as gathering wisdom from all sources, so when it is put into trial implementation, it is not completely satisfactory. It is difficult to avoid the feeling of building a car behind closed doors and not being able to adapt to the situation. Now that the Chinese Educational Society is established, it can truly be the largest advisory body to help the administrative side. In the future, it should cooperate with the administrative side practically. He hopes that the association will be an educational experimental institution, because the educational society has a plan for three kinds of experimental work, requesting experiments: (1) Mass education, (2) Industrial science experiment (3) Primary school production education experiment, (industrial science refers to agricultural and industrial production experiments in rural normal schools). Therefore, he hopes that this association will have three points: (1) I hope to be the central organization for education experiments, (2) I hope to be a government consultant advisory or suggestion organization (3) I hope to expand the organization, on the one hand, increase the strength to produce greater effects, and at the same time, I can gather more experts to study various professional problems separately. The experiment of primary school production education has also been entrusted to several places to handle, but the situation of its work has not been reported to the committee. New York Museum of Natural History Sends Personnel to Sichuan and Xikang to Collect Specimens

Overseas Chinese American Yang Dize to Depart Tomorrow Morning

Overseas Chinese American Yang Dize, commissioned by the American Museum of Natural History in New York, is scheduled to depart from Shanghai tomorrow morning aboard the Minsheng Shipping Company's Yongnian steamer. He will travel to Sichuan, Xikang, Qinghai, Gansu, and other provinces to collect specimens of flora and fauna. He will also cooperate with the Natural History Museum of the Academia Sinica in China in collecting these specimens. A reporter from the Central News Agency interviewed Mr. Yang at his Shanghai residence yesterday and learned the following details:

A Year-Long Journey Yang Dize's ancestral home is in Guangdong. He grew up in the United States and therefore holds American citizenship. For the past five years, he has traveled back and forth between China and the United States. Two years ago, he ventured alone into Tibet, Xinjiang, and other provinces to explore and collect numerous animal specimens. This time, representing both the American Museum of Natural History in New York City and the Natural History Museum of the Academia Sinica in China, he will travel to Xikang, Sichuan, Qinghai, and other provinces to collect specimens. The trip is scheduled to last one year, but he hopes to complete the assigned work within ten months, so he expects to return to Shanghai around November of this year.

Planned Route The route for this trip has already been planned. After arriving in Chongqing from Shanghai on the Yongnian steamer, he will switch to a boat to Ziyang. From Ziyang, he will travel overland through Ya'an to the Jinsha River area. He will then travel north into Qinghai and arrive in Gansu. He plans to stay in Xikang, Qinghai, and Gansu to collect specimens of flora and fauna. He will then take the Longhai Railway from Lanzhou back to Shanghai. After arriving in Shanghai, he will hand over the collected specimens of flora and fauna to the Academia Sinica first. The museum will keep those specimens it does not already have, and the rest will be taken back to the United States by Mr. Yang to report on his mission.

Accompanying Personnel In addition to his wife, Mr. Yang will be accompanied by his younger brother, Di Lin. Their passports and other documents are all prepared. He also carries a letter of introduction from Cai Yuanpei, the president of the Academia Sinica. Besides luggage, Mr. Yang's party is carrying a six-inch handgun, one hundred and fifty rounds of ammunition, and three shotguns with three hundred and fifty thousand rounds of ammunition. They have also obtained a transport permit from the National Government military authorities.

Promoting Social Education Should Focus on the National Language

(Nanjing, 25th) The Ministry of Education, based on a submission from the National Guoyu (National Language) Education Promotion Association, requests that all provincial and municipal education departments and bureaus, when promoting social education, should focus on the National Language. The measures are as follows: (1) Staff members of all levels of educational institutions who are handling social education must recognize and pay attention to phonetic symbols and be able to write in the National Language; otherwise, they will not be employed. (2) People's schools should first teach phonetic symbols to help with literacy. (3) People's reading materials and various official announcements should use the National Language. Phonetic symbols should be added to the edited text and news as appropriate. (4) Public places such as people's schools, education halls, libraries, and reading rooms should purchase Guoyu charts, phonetic books and newspapers, phonetic symbol machines, and other materials to display and promote their study and use.

Shanghai Municipal Council Distributes Winter School Subsidies

For the year 1933, 83 private Chinese schools within the Public Settlement have been approved by the Shanghai Municipal Council to receive subsidies. Shanghai Municipal Council Reviews Budget of Chinese Schools

The draft budget for this year for the Shanghai Municipal Council's five private Chinese primary schools, five Chinese middle schools for boys and girls, one normal school, and the Chinese Education Office has been submitted to the Education Committee. After discussion, the Committee decided to remove several items from the proposed additions, such as radio equipment, film preservation cabinets, and counting machines. It also requested the Director of Education to further reduce the number of experimental laboratory instruments and specimens. Other items can be listed as they are and transferred to the Finance Committee for review. This case has been submitted to the Board of Directors at its meeting on Wednesday for approval and record.

Attention Students' Families of Municipal Schools

Official Receipts Required for Fee Payments

Announcement Issued by the Municipal Education Bureau Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau announced yesterday: "It has been found that municipal primary schools, middle schools, and kindergartens in this city collect tuition and construction fees from students. According to the accounting regulations of this city, one copy of the official four-part receipt co-printed by this Bureau and the Finance Bureau must be issued to be considered legal. This Bureau has issued a notice to all municipal schools to comply with this regulation from the second semester of this year. It is also being announced in the newspapers, urging all parents of students in municipal schools to pay attention when paying tuition and construction fees. They must obtain the official four-part receipt co-printed by this Bureau and the Finance Bureau from the school. This is of utmost importance."

County Education Bureau Withholds January Funds for Guantao Elementary School

Due to Unclear Handover by Former Principal

Wang Shengfu (also known as Wang Boying), the principal of Guantao Primary School in the Second District of Shanghai County, was dismissed by order of the Education Bureau due to unsatisfactory school management as determined by the bureau's inspection. He Yunwen was appointed as the new principal. The new principal, He, accompanied by Huang Zhenzhong, a representative from the Education Bureau, went to the school yesterday to take over. However, Wang Shengfu not only failed to provide a clear inventory of the school's equipment and books but also refused to hand over the school seal. As a result, the new principal's handover was unsuccessful. Currently, to rectify the situation, the Education Bureau has decided to temporarily withhold the school's January funds until the handover is clear.

Philippine Chinese Chamber of Commerce Notifies All to Reject Donations Solicited in the Philippines

Municipal Education Bureau Instructs All Agencies and Schools to Take Note

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued the following instruction to all its affiliated schools and agencies yesterday: "A letter from the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Manila, Philippines, states: 'To whom it may concern, in recent years, business in the Philippines has been declining daily. Chinese merchants, both large and small, are in precarious situations and struggling to survive. However, those who come to the Philippines to solicit donations from the mainland are arriving one after another, even more than before. Given this situation, if we do not carefully consider and control the situation, currency will flow out, and the markets will become empty, leading to a continuous decline and eventual ruin. Considering this, to protect the position of the Chinese community in the Philippines, this Chamber convened a joint meeting on December 5th with the Chinese Educational Association, the Chinese Benevolent Society, and various Chinese trade associations. They all agreed that it is necessary to sympathize with the difficult times and stop donating money to allow for recovery and benefit trade. It was decided that 'starting from next year (1934), all those who come to the Philippines to solicit donations from the mainland will be rejected. If necessary, a joint meeting of the above-mentioned organizations will be convened to resolve the matter.' Based on this, we hereby record the case and instruct you to take note and inform all local agencies and organizations. If anyone intends to go abroad to solicit donations, they should not go to the Philippines to avoid unnecessary travel and wasted time.'"

Jinan University Student School Protection Committee Holds Meeting

Shanghai News reports: Since the Ministry of Education decided on the handling of the Jinan University incident, the university's Student School Protection Committee held its fifth meeting yesterday. The meeting was chaired by Zhou Shifu, and the following important resolutions were made: (1) Regarding the reported announcement by the Ministry of Education that Shen Pengfei will be appointed as the acting president of the university, how should this committee respond? It was decided to discuss this further after the official order arrives. (2) Regarding the reinstatement of all students who were unfairly expelled and teachers and staff who were unfairly dismissed, it was decided to pass the motion. (3) Regarding the reduction of tuition, boarding, and miscellaneous fees to ease the financial burden on students, it was decided that (a) university tuition should be standardized with Central University, with equal treatment for new and old students; (b) middle school tuition should be standardized based on the resolutions passed by the middle school general assembly. (4) Regarding the improvement of the curriculum organization, with one clock hour as one credit, it was decided to pass the motion. (5) Regarding the motion proposed by first-year students to refund the 20 yuan paid for the gymnasium construction fee last semester, it was decided to pass the motion. (6) Regarding the organization of a drafting committee for suggestions on improving Jinan University's administration, it was decided that each of the university, middle school, and overseas student associations should nominate two people to form the committee. The standing committee of the School Protection Committee will collect suggestions from all students and submit them to the committee for inclusion in the suggestions. Additionally, the Shanghai alumni of Jinan University held a meeting yesterday, chaired by Qiu Hanping. The principles for deciding on suggestions for reforming Jinan University were: (1) the principles of overseas Chinese education; (2) the development of national culture; (3) the training of student spirit; and (4) the reform of school administration. Ping Zuren and four others were nominated as members of the drafting committee, which is scheduled to meet on Saturday to present the suggestions for approval.

May 30th Cemetery Board of Directors Actively Prepares to Establish Elementary School

Reappoints Lin Kanghou as Convener of the Education Division

Rejects Municipal Qiandong Elementary School's Request to Borrow Memorial Hall

The May 30th Cemetery Board of Directors decided during last year's public memorial service to establish the May 30th Elementary School in the cemetery's memorial hall to commemorate the event permanently. Recently, the board held another meeting and reappointed Lin Kanghou as the convener of the education division. The Municipal Qiandong Elementary School's request to borrow the cemetery's memorial hall as a school building was politely rejected. The board's original letters to Lin Kanghou and the Municipal Education Bureau are recorded below:

Letter to Lin Kanghou: "To whom it may concern, the matter of establishing the May 30th Elementary School in the May 30th Cemetery Memorial Hall for permanent commemoration was decided during the May 30th public memorial service in 1933. It has now been resolved at the 11th Board of Directors meeting of the May 30th Cemetery on the 23rd of this month that the school will be established and operated starting in 1934. Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Cheng Xiechun, Yuan Ludeng, Zhao Jinqing, Gu Xinyi, Wang Hanliang, and Wu Zhihao have been publicly nominated as school directors, with Director Lin Kanghou as the convener of the board. The original education division of the board consisted of Directors Chen Dezheng, Zhao Jinqing, and Gu Xinyi, with Director Chen Dezheng as the convener. Director Chen has not attended meetings for a long time, so the position of convener of the education division has been reassigned to Director Lin Kanghou. The education division will be responsible for preparing all matters related to the May 30th Elementary School, aiming to open the school at the beginning of the fall semester this year. A request should be submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau for record. We hereby inform you of this matter and hope that you will accept the position. Sincerely, May 30th Cemetery Board of Directors."

Letter to the Education Bureau: "To the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, we are writing in response to the letter delivered by Directors Wang Xiaolai and Cheng Xiechun regarding the Municipal Qiandong Elementary School's proposal to borrow the May 30th Memorial Hall as a school building. It was decided during the May 30th public memorial service in 1933 that the May 30th Elementary School would be established to commemorate the event permanently. It was also resolved at the 11th Board of Directors meeting of the May 30th Cemetery that Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Cheng Xiechun, Yuan Ludeng, Zhao Jinqing, Gu Xinyi, Wang Hanliang, and Wu Zhihao would be publicly nominated as school directors, with Director Lin Kanghou as the convener. All preparations will be carried out by the education division of the May 30th Cemetery Board of Directors, and the school is scheduled to open at the beginning of the fall semester this year. All of this is recorded. Therefore, the request to borrow the hall for Qiandong Elementary School cannot be granted. We respectfully request that you take note and reply accordingly. Sincerely, May 30th Cemetery Board of Directors."
