Free Talk

Continuing the Discussion on "Shanghai Style"

— Cao Juren

Mr. Shen Congwen defines "Shanghai Style" as "the combination of a scholar's talent and sentiment with commercial competition, thus establishing our current concept of the term 'Shanghai Style.'" Mr. Xu Maoyong raises an objection, believing that "if there truly is a distinction between 'Shanghai Style' and 'Beijing Style' in the literary world, then I believe commercial competition is a characteristic of the former, while a scholar's talent and sentiment are characteristics of the latter." This made me recall a passage from Mr. Lu Xun's lecture on a glimpse of Shanghai literature and art. When the Shanghai foreign settlement was first opened, talented scholars, often melancholic and sickly, came from all over. They regarded Zhang Garden as the Grand View Garden and the prostitutes as the Twelve Beauties of Jinling, believing that "only talented scholars can pity these fallen beauties, and only beauties can recognize the unfortunate scholars," thus becoming like celestial couples. Unfortunately, they later "discovered that the beauties did not become prostitutes out of a thirst for talent but purely for money. They felt it was unacceptable for the beauties to want money from the talented scholars, so they devised various ingenious methods to subdue the prostitutes, not only avoiding being tricked but also taking advantage of them." Therefore, the initial form of Shanghai Style was talented scholars plus fools, which later progressed to become talented scholars plus hooligans.

In a shop window in East Xinqiao, there is a painting with the famous line "The Eight Immortals Playing Mahjong" inscribed on it. Of course, it should also have a painting of "The Eight Immortals Hunting Pheasant" to make it perfect, but we are already satisfied. It interprets the meaning of "Shanghai Style" more clearly than thousands of words. The Eight Immortals are so pure and lofty, so detached from the mundane world; but once they arrive in the foreign settlement, they cannot help but "modernize" and live a "mahjong-playing" life. We ordinary people are even more likely to do so. The imposing Lake Society next to Stealing Chicken Bridge was formerly the famous Shou Sheng Nunnery. According to investigations, in the secret chambers, in addition to various cosmetics, there are also substances like white turbid powder. In the west gate, there is a grand residence with many wives and concubines, whose master is the abbot of a certain mountain. The one who performed rituals at the Great World in 1933 was none other than Zhang, the Heavenly Master, who had left Longhu Mountain. This Shanghai foreign settlement has its own greatness. Any powerful demon, no matter what kind of disguise it wears, whether it is a Taoist robe, a Buddhist cassock, or a long gown and mandarin jacket, will eventually reveal its true form in this large mirror, with a long tail dragging behind it.

Writers and artists, though also fox spirits who have cultivated themselves for thousands of years, have beautiful patterns such as "morality," "purity," and "spiritual life" embroidered on their outer garments; however, in the "mirror that reveals demons," their true forms are still revealed. From the perspective of the Beijing Style, this is of course a bit glaring, with such a long tail dragging outside the outer garment. But what can be done? This is where the divergence between "Beijing Style" and "Shanghai Style" comes in: knowing that it cannot be concealed, simply drag the tail out, this is "Shanghai Style"; twisting and turning, still trying to lengthen the outer garment and cover the tail, this is "Beijing Style." The sage said: Better "Shanghai Style" than "Beijing Style." It is always too tiring to constantly pay attention to the hem of the outer garment. In the terminology of Shanghai Style, there are so-called X-style and Y-style things, such as a 1934-style car, a 1934-style cheongsam, which in commercial competition, is called "market price." Unfortunately, the 1933-style Shanghai Style writer has been kicked out of the commercial competition market; new books are weighed and priced by the pound, and friends who solicit manuscripts can hardly even afford the northwest wind. The characteristic of merely "commercial competition" has also been crossed out. Looking at it this way, the 1934-style Shanghai Style writer is not enough with "talented scholar" plus "hooligan," there should be another kind of addition; unfortunately, I don't understand mathematics, I don't know how the formula in "Euclidean" geometry should be arranged!

Going to the Yi Regions

— Liu Ming

"Men go to the Yi regions, women often remain widows. If they return alive, they bring epidemics; if they die, they are abandoned by the roadside."

Listening to the temporary travel companions, dragging out their voices, singing the folk songs of the Zhendongzhou people, a wisp of melancholy quietly wrapped around my heart. Following them as they turned down the hillside, I felt as if I lacked the strength that a traveler should have.

At the foot of the slope, a narrow, elongated wilderness, misty and desolate, stretched out to the gray horizon. This was the Yi region I was about to journey to, the miasmic and rainy Yi region.

High mountains, dark and gloomy high mountains, with white mists like turbans on their heads, stretched along both sides of the wilderness, appearing savage and fierce. In those white mists on the mountaintops, the homes of the wild people were hidden. Their lives, it was said, consisted of coming down the mountains to plunder the Bai Yi people in the wilderness and passing travelers.

At that time, it was probably past Qingming (Tomb-Sweeping Day). In the Han regions, it was still a warm spring, but here (called the Yi Fang Ba by the Yunnan people, and written as Ganya in the Yuan History) it was already like summer, with a stifling heat everywhere: the heat of the mist, the heat of the rain, the heat of the humidity.

My travel companion (a middle-aged man) said that before Qingming and up until September of last year, there was no shortage of sunny days here. There was a good sun every day, and you wouldn't see a single drop of rain. But now, we're out of luck. It rains several times every day. The rain here is not like the rain in the Han regions, it's poisonous and terrifying (you can easily get sick). And then there's the miasma, the miasma! God bless us! As he said this, his whole body trembled as if he had been suddenly attacked. He immediately rebuked me kindly, saying that as a young man, why didn't I come out in the twelfth lunar month? Was I here to die now?

As I listened to him, I saw the Bai Yi women on the road. Many of them had clear brows and bright eyes, and some of the farm girls were even more beautiful than Han Chinese women. So I said, aren't the people here living well?

"These are Yi people!" he retorted loudly; immediately citing many terrible cases of Han people getting miasma poisoning here. I had nothing to say, so I used one sentence to counter him, which was to say, then what are you doing in the Yi region now?

"Oh God, it's to earn a living, to support my family," he groaned in distress. Because I wanted to win the argument, I replied with a smile: "Aren't I the same as you?" In fact, at that time, I had no family, nor was I only working to support myself; most of the reason was because I was tired of the reality of my environment, so I wandered around like a gypsy. However, in order to see novel sights, I had come to such a discouraging place, so naturally, I couldn't help but feel a little melancholy.

"Then, are you doing the same kind of business as me?" he asked, his eyes flashing cunningly.

"What? What business are you doing?" I asked him.

"Er... er..." he didn't answer, just humming his folk song of the Zhendongzhou people.

Later, when we reached the Ba Mu wilderness and were searched by plainclothes Burmese police, I learned that he, my very good travel companion, was smuggling opium. If I had known earlier, I would have put on the same mature expression as him and offered my advice like he rebuked me. But he, along with the contraband, was taken to prison that time, and I never saw him again.

Shanghai-Nanjing Express - Black Baby

Woo... woo... woo...

The steam whistle howls. The locomotive, bulging its belly, charges forward, black smoke billowing straight up, trailing behind it in the wind.

Mountains, fields, and forests all recede.

Looking from afar, the train resembles a long snake. 'Ker-thump... ker-thump...' the rhythmically clanging wheels keep turning non-stop: Shanghai-Nanjing Express!

In the first-class carriage:

Spacious, clean, comfortable…

With a high-priced cigar in his mouth, standing by the glass looking at the scenery outside the train; in this "dignitary's" heart: 'It's winter, the beautiful fields are all withered and yellow.' His daughter throws aside a novel and relaxes. She looks at her father and, after a while, speaks:

'Dad, I'm not going back when we get to Shanghai!' 'What are you saying? What do you plan to do in Shanghai?'

'Study.'

'You can study in Nanjing. Why?'

'Isn't Shanghai better?... Sigh, let's talk about it slowly. Dad, I'm a bit hungry, let's order something to eat!'

Having said that, she stretches lazily and "ha"-s, exhaling.

Then, fifteen minutes later, a lot of things are brought.

While eating, the daughter smiles and strokes the "dignitary's" face.

In the second-class carriage:

Dragon Well tea, melon seeds, tabloids…

A section chief half-lying in his seat, reading a tabloid. He is middle-aged and sports a small mustache. A woman and her husband, sitting opposite him, both look tired, their eyes closed, dozing off. The section chief's eyes slip over from the newspaper. They linger on the woman's delicate face for a minute or two. Suddenly, the steam whistle howls again, the woman opens her eyes, and the section chief quickly looks back at the newspaper.

The woman takes a sip of Dragon Well tea.

The husband is sleeping like a pig. She glances indifferently at her slightly plump husband and shakes her head.

As the section chief changes to another newspaper, he thinks to himself: 'Not bad, this woman is desirable! But…' and touches the mustache on his lip.

In the third-class carriage:

Long gowns, melon-cap hats, noisy voices…

A Jiangbei woman, in such cold weather, bares her breasts to feed her child. A layer of darkness covers her face…

Suddenly, the child abandons the nipple and starts crying, crying loudly. A man wearing a melon-cap hat, sitting not far away, grumbles:

"Damn it! What are you crying for? Damn it…"

But how could the child understand people's annoyance? He continues to cry loudly, crying.

Noisy, clamorous,…

Women, children, men,…

The ticket inspector walks past here, followed by armed soldiers. An old man, seeing them pass, begins to talk to his daughter-in-law:

'The last time I went to Shanghai, I traveled fourth class… You don't know, the people in fourth class are all like pigs, so pitiful, so… That time, there were two poor people who didn't have money to buy tickets and were almost thrown off halfway! I saw them crying and even pleaded on their behalf to the ticket inspector!'

Shanghai-Nanjing Express! The rhythmically clanging wheels keep turning non-stop: 'Ker-thump... ker-thump!...' Looking from afar, the train resembles a long snake.

Mountains, fields, and forests all recede.

The steam whistle howls. The locomotive, bulging its belly, charges forward, black smoke billowing straight up, trailing behind it in the wind.

Woo… woo… woo…

On "Jealousy" (Continued)

— Shi Heng

The simplicity of the plot, especially the focus on the theme of jealousy, can easily make us think that the play will be lengthy, rambling, and tedious. But Pierre Hamp, worthy of being the son of the homeland of modern drama, writes very well. Through extremely appropriate and concise dialogue, he keeps the entire play developing tightly until the end, without paralyzing the characters due to the excessive expression of psychology, and without making the dialogue fall into looseness or tedium due to the scarcity of concrete facts. Although only four characters appear, he arranges them very well, with no unnecessary appearances and very few unnecessary words.

But if we examine it from an ideological perspective, the author commits the mistake of a vague consciousness. He sets the event against the backdrop of World War I, and the characters are also heavily influenced by the devastation of the war. However, he places the husband's jealousy under a generalized situation for a deep explanation. Although the words of this unfortunate couple occasionally reveal that the war destroyed this young man and caused their lives to suffer misfortune, the author certainly did not explain that the general public's disillusionment with hope and weariness of life after the war led to this morbid psychological suspicion. This fact can be proven by Blanche's thoughts and words. She says: "His country is attracting me. It is as if a door has suddenly opened, and from this door, I see a path that I have been seeking for a long time... Perhaps it is happiness." After the war, the countries of Germany, Austria, and France were destroyed, but only the United States was able to maintain a new and prosperous capitalist country. Europeans, looking at the tragic scenes around them after the war, could not help but yearn for the flourishing America. Blanche's remarks are merely representative of the general opinion of Europeans. However, in this play, the author says that it is because of the husband's unreasonable jealousy that she feels disillusioned, feels the ruthlessness of daily life, and endures the pain of abandoning her beloved person to run to a strange land.

In order to make the husband's jealousy a powerful reason for destroying their happy life, the author feels very difficult, especially because this is in dramatic literature, and this difficulty is shown very clearly. He painstakingly and meticulously uses the methods of French naturalism to dissect the psychology of jealousy, in order to make up for the development of events and show unnatural traces. But he ultimately cannot find a particularly appropriate reason, but only the old explanation of the conflict between love and jealousy. The impact of the war is only ancillary. He has André say: "I love you too much, I will love you more appropriately in the future. I don't know how to love you properly now. What returned to you from the Darmstadt camp was a barbarian, a person ruined by suffering." And, "... a kind of sinister suspicion sometimes covers my reason. It is just like an irresistible fever that is infected in people. If I didn't love you so much, it wouldn't have come to this. Ah! Forgive me!..." At the same time, in order to give André's jealousy a considerable basis, the author further arranged an anecdote, that is, the matter of the wife's friend, Jeanne. When André was in captivity, one of his companions named Weber died. At the time of his death, he revealed this secret to André - the secret love between Weber and Jeanne. André, due to the shock this matter gave him, later reasoned: "This man thought his woman was pure, and I also thought my woman was pure." "This man never left his woman. Me, I was away from home for four years." In this way, her jealousy seemed even more reasonable.

But, no matter how the author tries to make up for it, how he wants to convince the reader of the reason for jealousy destroying life, we can see another truth from the events he describes - if that is a faithful depiction of reality - that a powerful reason that destroyed their happy life. That is, the inevitable decline of their lives was bestowed by the war and determined by their era. For example, André, after returning home after four years of captivity, even if his wife did not give him any cause for suspicion, would they have lived happily together? That would also have been impossible. (To be continued)

Father and Daughter (7)

— Jin Yi

"Excuse me, Miss, I'm disturbing you."

The female guest was so humble, so polite, and her voice was so pleasant. She deliberately took a step or two, gazing at the portrait hanging in the study. She knew her eyes were not mistaken. Her heart was pounding. She said to the woman, "Please sit down. You can take off your coat first."

Seeing the female guest take off her coat, she went over to take it and hung it on the coat rack behind the door. The female guest sat down, and she herself sat in the seat opposite.

The maid brought two cups of tea, placing them in front of them.

"Do you live in this city?"

"No, I'm just passing through. Once, oh, once I lived here too."

"Did you come to this city specifically to play?"

"Not really, I'm with my husband…"

The female guest stopped suddenly when she got to this point, as if something had grabbed her heart, and a little embarrassment was revealed. Seeing this, she let her drink some tea, and seeing her pick up the tea, she herself also raised the teacup to her lips. "We're going to X, passing through here, we'll only stay for two or three days."

After the female guest finished speaking, she fixed her eyes on a piece of plain silk hanging on the wall, on which were embroidered four lines of poetry about love between men and women. She remembered seeing that strange decoration when she was very young. She took a cigarette from her cigarette case and offered it to the female guest. "Would you like a cigarette?"

"Thank you."

Because she was watching so intently, she was startled by her words, and she thanked her a little flusteredly. She struck a match and lit the cigarette for the guest. The female guest seemed very skilled and cleverly held the cigarette between the index and middle fingers of her right hand, which showed that she was a fan of cigarettes.

"Do you have something important to see my father about?"

"Nothing, just came to see him. He's an old friend of mine."

"Oh, is that so!——"

She deliberately prolonged her voice.

"How has he been lately?"

"Very good, everything is fine,——"

Tea Exported in the 22nd Year

｜Published by the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau: 11% Increase Compared to the Previous Year｜

Customs figures for tea trade in the 22nd year have not yet been released, but a comparison of the export inspection numbers from the Shanghai and Hankou Commodity Inspection Bureaus reveals that they have

exceeded the 21st year by 11%. The prices of black tea from Hubei and Hunan were also higher than in the 21st year. Although Ping-Shui and Huizhou green teas fell by 40%, they remained stable with little fluctuation. Therefore, those engaged in sales and management in the 22nd year, except for the significant losses in Qimen tea and some unfavorable situations in Jiangxi Ninghong tea, mostly had some remaining profits to be made.

Amidst the global economic panic, the export of all products has suffered a severe decline. The fact that the tea industry can exhibit this phenomenon is not to be considered an unsatisfactory outcome. Enclosed is a table of the quantities of black tea, green tea, and brick tea exported to various countries in the last two years (unit: dan).

The brick tea category is completely dominated by Russia. The increase/decrease numbers are detailed in the previous table. However, the increase in black tea is mostly low-grade tea from Hubei and Hunan. Other teas exported to Russia include a small amount of rough tea and a

batch of scented tea, which is the latest type of tea imported by Russia.

Indica Rice: Near-Term Futures Fall, Long-Term Rise

Wheat Futures Show Little Fluctuation

After the market opened yesterday morning, due to the factory's previous two boatloads of wheat sold on credit, the market sentiment had softened. Additionally, shipments of fixed-price wheat were arriving continuously, with two new shipments expected by the end of the month. Small factories were making purchases of foreign wheat and

immediately hedging in the market. Large factories were taking a wait-and-see approach, but not taking advantage of small dips to cover their positions. Short-term speculative traders, considering the situation of the factories, were also selling at any time. However, while short-term speculative traders and retail investors were selling near-month contracts, they were buying back long-term contracts. Therefore, the longer-term months rebounded after a period of weakness, while near-month contracts lacked covering demand, and bulls were eager to sell. With small factories also hedging, the market could not hold steady. The closing price for this month was down 1.25 points, February and March were each down 0.25 points, April was up 0.5 points, May was up 2.5 points, and June was up 7.5 points.

There were no spot transactions for wheat, and inventory was low. Asking prices still ranged from $4.10 to $4.15. Wheat futures saw very little trading volume throughout the day due to year-end settlements, with neither side actively participating. Market prices showed little fluctuation, with the closing price down only 0.01 points for the current month, and minimal changes for other months.

Increased Price of Guest Indica Rice Leads to Sluggish Sales

Yesterday, landlords of Guest Indica rice, noting the smooth sales of Kehua rice and limited arrivals, raised prices by 0.10 dollars. As a result, the Fujian traders reduced their purchases, with only over 200 bags of Nanjing machine indica rice transacted. Both local merchants and rural estates inquired about prices. Yesterday's market saw the transaction of 200 bags of Hunan machine oil rice at $7.10, 100 bags of Jiangxi machine late rice at $7.25, 25 bags of machine Yuan rice at $6.50, and 300 bags of Nanjing machine rice at prices ranging from $6.28 to $6.09, similar to the previous market.

Abundant Arrivals of Late Rice

｜Thick粳 Rice Sales Sluggish, Prices Slightly Lower｜

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, a total of over 80 shipments arrived from various origins, amounting to over 10,000 piculs, with late rice accounting for half of the total. Fortunately, the outgoing path for wholesalers turned active, so the market conditions did not show much decline. However, goods such as Qingjiao, Songjiang, Sixi, and Xilian rice, and the 3,000 plus bags delivered by the Northern Tianjin Tanggu traders, the Southern Xiamen traders, and upper-tier warehouses saw a slight adjustment of 0.06 dollars. Due to the relatively abundant arrivals of thick 粳 rice from various traders, the local shop wholesalers became less active, and the market conditions softened by several cents, approaching a dime. Duyang tip rice, on the other hand, did not show excessive fluctuations, and both Yinbian and Yuan rice were seen to be turning fixed.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, 35-36 shipments arrived from various routes along the river. The outflow of various goods in the market was average, and the prices of high-quality white 粳 rice and white Yuan rice were firm. Medium and lower grades saw slight price declines of nearly a dime, while Yangdu Bujian rice also showed a softening trend. Early thin rice and Yin Yuan guest tip rice were firm.

Miscellaneous Grains Push Peanuts Higher

Due to the Impending Lunar New Year

Yesterday, spot transactions of miscellaneous grains were unusually scattered. Total transactions for all grains in the market did not exceed 3,000 bags. For soybeans, two truckloads of Zhengyangguan beans, two truckloads of Yingzhou beans, and one truckload of Bengbu beans were offered, with no price changes. Wholesalers from inland areas and local merchants purchased them. The remaining Niuzhuang red sorghum was offered at 500 bags, priced at $3.02. Kaiyuan corn was offered at 110 bags, priced at $3.05. Nanjing Minglu green beans were offered at 150 bags, priced at $3.47. Tancheng raw red peanuts were offered at 110 bags, priced at $5.10. Shuanggou peanuts were offered at 300 bags, priced at $6.30. Market prices, except for the rising peanuts and the weakening raw kernels, remained generally stable.

Sugar Market: Red and White Sugar Clearing Prices Rise Again

Chaoqing Sugar Opens Lower

Yesterday, the sugar market saw rising customs gold and standard gold prices, and a slight contraction in Dutch exchange rates, leading to a tighter trend. The association clearing price for 24 grade coarse sand white common goods was $19.70, an increase of $0.10 from the previous day. Transit goods were $6.70, an increase of $0.15 from Tuesday. Dutch red Gao Chen goods were cleared at $16.20, an increase of $0.20. New Gao goods were quoted at $15.85, and new lower-grade goods were cleared at $15.45. Taikoo sugar tightened further yesterday, with quotations up $0.30. B Mark was quoted at $20.30, but no transaction was made. Zhenyu No. 1 reduced white rose another $0.10 to $18.90. Numbers 2, 3, and 4 each retreated $0.20 per grade. Changxing Trading Company continued to offer over 3,000 bags of Zhengmian Dutch white sugar, still at $19.00, but refused to offer further, taking a tight view on the lower market. There were more upper-grade Chaoqing sugar than lower-grade sugar, so market trends varied depending on the quantity. 200 plus bags were offered yesterday, priced at $12.20 to $12.00, and lower-grade sugar was priced at $11.45 to $11.20, down $0.23 to $0.12 from the previous day. Hainan red Xushengji offered over 200 bags, priced at $13.65.

Talking Points

Year of Peace

— Lizhai

The famous prophetic Mrs. Bones has recently, with her insightful prophetic vision, said that

1934 will be a "Year of Peace" with "absolutely no wars." It is inherently as difficult for all prophets to "speak subtly and hit the mark" about world affairs as winning first or second prize in an aviation lottery. However, regarding the "Year of Peace" that Mrs. Bones is spouting nonsense about (whether it is "as if echoing sound" or has no efficacy, the words of any prophet cannot escape the category of "spouting nonsense"), I believe that, apart from our noble nation fundamentally being listed as an exception, there is a degree of objective possibility in the extrapolation of international trends, for the following reasons:

First, esteemed readers have likely watched at least one or two "National Operas." Those who have watched National Opera will definitely not forget: Whenever "Golden Leopard," "Antian Assembly," "Changban Slope," and other "stage is filled with fire," "heavenly soldiers and generals" "full martial arts" scenes appear, there must be two or three minutes of tranquility on stage, the curtain is lowered, intermittent gongs are struck, and the stagehands clear the tables and chairs, changing the battle scene, clearing space, so that those martial artists can "wrestle barehanded" and "fight with weapons." After these procedures are completed, only then are the gongs and drums beaten loudly, waiting for the generals and soldiers to rush out, point generals, assemble formations, and start fighting... gradually intensifying the performance. The current international stage is also like the stage of our noble nation's national opera, just temporarily quiet to clear the stage before the "full martial arts" are performed. Although international wars are absolutely inevitable, the imperialist powers almost all have something to wait for. Jin Yuan Guo, on the one hand, wants to be busy finding a way to recover from the Blue Eagle Movement, and on the other hand, wants to wait for the completion of the one hundred and one major warship construction plans. Wooden Clog Country must calmly digest Manchuria, and also complete its "emergency time plan" before 1936 in terms of military and political aspects. Other countries such as Britain, France, and Italy are all frantically preparing for war on the one hand, and doing everything possible in diplomatic alliances on the other hand. In addition to this, various conferences to do what humans can are to be held, and "

Peace" is to be advocated. Therefore, judging from the extrapolation of various facts, it is not entirely a fantasy to say that this year can become a "Year of Peace."

Second, if we want to make the "Year of Peace" a "domestic product," I am afraid that there will be very few days possible. Because among our compatriots who like to play with guns and cannons, the warlords in Fujian Province last year killed and slashed a lot, creating a full martial arts performance, eager to play, and this year it seems that the excitement has not subsided, and "continued efforts are still needed." Don't you see Sun Dianying and Ma Hongkui? Now they have the determination to "destroy this dynasty for food" and are doing the opposite work of "Year of Peace." Therefore, apart from a few important people who will again

"go abroad" (Chen Zhenru and Li Renchao will probably have to "go abroad" this year), most of the groups of Adou (foolish sons), mostly will not have the blessing of enjoying the "Year of Peace."

Third, superstitious things like prophecies are most popular in our China, but are rarely seen in the countries of foreign adults. However, the Year of Peace that Mrs. Bones recently spouted nonsense about has caused a sensation in various countries, attracting attention. What is the reason for this? Because humanity's immersion in superstition becomes more profound when faced with turbulent times. When the world is full of waves and disaster lies in ambush everywhere, the encounters and experiences of life often reach the extreme of strangeness and change, and it is extremely difficult to grasp and control them according to one's own will. Thus, many people who run into walls in human affairs and become "monks who are two feet tall and unable to figure things out" unconsciously seek spiritual comfort from the aspect of "destiny" from subjective depression. The increasing popularity of Chinese astrology and the widespread attention drawn by Western prophecies are both for this reason. The imperialists, whose heads are dizzy from war crises and economic panic, also want to think about what "destiny" is like outside of "human affairs."

Although the "Year of Peace" is the advance team of the "Year of Great War," the world, which is deeply worried about war, is happy to hear the prophecy of the "Year of Peace." In that case, Mrs. Bones, in this year of multiple difficulties, is also a "gospel messenger" who temporarily anesthetizes.

Words on Warming by the Fire

— Dao

On cold days, people cannot avoid warming themselves by the fire. This act of warming by the fire was probably passed down from distant ancestors and existed in ancient times. However, in modern times, with the prosperity of science, the method of heating with steam pipes and water radiators has defeated the "ancient method" of warming by the fire. Although this is a lament for the decline of ancient customs in the sense of preserving national essence, it is also fortunate for the rapid progress in the enjoyment of human happiness. As for the method of warming with steam pipes and water radiators, it can only be enjoyed by a few people in big cities, so let's not talk about it for now. Let's talk about warming by the fire now.

Those who can install a stove at home to warm themselves by the fire are naturally not as wealthy as those who install steam pipes and water radiators at home, but "it is better to be below than above," and warming by the stove is, after all, much warmer than installing a brazier to warm oneself. Those who can install a brazier at home to warm themselves by the fire are naturally not as good as those who install a stove at home, but it can also be said that it is "better to be below than above," and a brazier is still much warmer than freezing without a brazier. This kind of philosophy of life of "it is better to be below than above" is also called "contentment" and "keeping to one's fate," and should be "strictly obeyed." Therefore, I installed a brazier at home, feeling content and living in peace.

But last night, before going to bed, I was greedily reading a beloved book in bed and forgot to extinguish the fire in the brazier. Under the attack of the toxic quality of carbon monoxide, I fell asleep drowsily and did not wake up until lunchtime today. After everyone knocked on the door and shouted loudly, I finally woke up a little like waking up from a dream. I almost suffocated to death in this small room with the windows and doors closed. | This is really because my fate is still good and my luck has not declined | At the same time, I saw in today's newspaper that a certain family's nanny died of suffocation from warming by the fire in a small room, which made me break out in a cold sweat. Because of my own near suffocation and the stimulus of knowing that someone had really suffocated to death from the newspaper report, I was temporarily blinded by greed and imagined that if everyone could enjoy steam pipes and water radiators ... Of course, this is a non-divisional thought, but in fact, this thought is not illegal. How can it be said that it is not illegal? The prosperity of science and the result of the shift of the times naturally lead to the electrification of cities progressing to the electrification of rural areas. Where electrification has already occurred, steam pipes and water radiators can naturally be installed for heating, but this era of electrification in both cities and rural areas is far, far away.

However, today's newspaper published a news item similar to a commentary called "Development of Home Electrification," saying, "For electricity, factories, transportation, and traffic, everyone is amazed by its wide use and its grand effect. However, in modern times, with the prosperity of science, the use of electricity... therefore, there is the realization of home electrification... Today, there are no less than tens of millions of such families being built, and it can be asserted that in the future, it will increase to hundreds of millions." Then, the era of "home electrification" that "will increase to hundreds of millions in the future" and is "assertable" is not too far away.

Winter Tonics

— Bao Xu

Once it's winter, the newspapers are filled with advertisements from pharmacies, saying that winter is the best time to take tonics, and everyone should take some tonics, which can eliminate diseases, prolong life, nourish Yang, and benefit longevity.

Of course, in these years, the national fortune is declining day by day. If everyone can take some tonics and everyone can eliminate diseases, prolong life, nourish Yang, and benefit longevity, this will have an indirect impact on the future of our nation, not to mention that our own bodies can be very strong, and if we have children, then our future children, because of heredity, will naturally all be as strong as us. Then, even if we are destroyed by the enemy, are we still afraid that our own children will always have a day to retaliate for this "irreconcilable" hatred? At that time, let us wait and see! I am afraid that those neighboring countries will say "the Yellow Peril" is coming again!

Therefore, there is really no difference between Chinese and Western culture. Although Hitler in Germany is now promoting eugenics and heredity, in China, we are also promoting it. However, there is some difference in the method. The Germans rule the world with "hegemony," while we Chinese rule the world with "benevolence." The only difference is in this!

Therefore, the appearance of tonics in such years, if we think about it with a little logic, who can say that it is not appropriate? I therefore look in the mirror every day to see my own face, feeling that it is almost getting yellower and thinner day by day, and I also quite want to take some tonics to replenish myself, and a few friends who care about me also advise me on this when they meet me. Those friends who understand Western medicine say, "You must get some blood-replenishing injections to make your body strong!" Those friends who understand Chinese medicine say, "You must eat some ginseng or deer antler to make your body strong!" And myself, after hearing their words, I can only respond with a smile.

Naturally, I thank them all for their kindness. Whether they advise me to get blood-replenishing injections or eat ginseng or deer antler, although the methods are different, the principle of replenishment is always the same, right?

However, at this winter season, people like me, or people who are not as good as me, the things they are worried about every day are not about the internal replenishment of the body, but about the external clothing of the body. "The whole family is in the wind, and the clothes for September have not been cut," this line of poetry coughed up from free blood, at this winter season, is it not protesting to the season for many people?

The reason why I smiled it off is right here.

Brother Mao and Sister Bao Travel the World

Novel

Manli's Freedom (7)

— Manzhi

He enjoyed reading newspapers, treating it as a kind of work.

"Didn't you say before that not reading newspapers calms the mind, but reading newspapers makes one crazy? Why do you enjoy

reading newspapers now?" I asked him this way.

"The previous concept was wrong. The more evil society is, the more we should face the evil of society. Newspapers tell us the evils of society, and we should study the root causes of the evils of society to see if the theory matches the facts, and then we can move forward to achieve success in theory and practice." He answered calmly like that.

He not only didn't drink alcohol, but he also didn't smoke cigarettes! The Jai Alai court was even more like a relic of the previous century to him.

Apart from teaching classes, he stayed at home reading books, writing manuscripts, or meeting guests and chatting. It was rare to see him go out, although you might still find him taking a walk in the park after dinner.

I occasionally asked him, "What about Manli?"

He just shook his head with a smile on his painful expression.

I regretted that I shouldn't have brought up his personal affairs and uncovered his wounds. I was afraid he would go crazy again, so I quickly changed the subject and talked to him about the weather being too cold that day. However, in my heart, I was asking myself, "He shook his head, what does that mean? Does it mean it's over? Does it mean he's already not thinking about it anymore?" I replied to myself in this way, "His heart has been bitten by the poisonous snake of sorrow, and even his heart is numb."

The second time I went to look for him, he disappeared!

Don't worry, listen to me tell you.

I went to look for him the day after he disappeared. As soon as I entered the door, your servant Ou asked me anxiously and busily,

"Mr. Chen, have you seen Mr. Tang?"

"No."

"He, he left the house yesterday and hasn't come home!"

"Hasn't come home?" I was shocked.

"Yes, hasn't come home. Usually, he doesn't leave the house all day on Monday, which I found strange

, unexpectedly, he still hasn't come home today!"

"Did he take anything with him?"

"No, he just left wearing an old cotton robe, without even changing out of his suit!"

He liked to wear that old cotton robe at home, saying that it was warmer than a suit, which I had seen, but he always changed into a suit before leaving the house, so why did he leave wearing that old cotton robe, and why hasn't he come home even now

? | I immediately became uneasy in my heart.

I called every place where his friends were to ask... they all said he hadn't come.

I told them all about his disappearance. Before long, his friends all came to your house.

Everyone kept questioning your servant Ou, but the servant Ou could only... a few... (the words are missing after that) ... Afterwards, he resigned and disappeared.

Movie Supplement

Literary Figures Value the Film Industry

— Chen Xiong

England and America Face Each Other Across the Ocean

Works of Equal Stature are Together Adapted for the Silver Screen

Regarding England: The British film industry, which closely follows America's Hollywood, has recently produced works that show a trend of surpassing it. Moreover, many Hollywood stars have been courted by the British film industry, with Douglas Fairbanks, Sr. and Jr. being the most notable. Douglas Fairbanks, Sr. has decided to produce films of the "Robin Hood" type in London, England, while Douglas Fairbanks, Jr. is currently filming "Catherine the Great". Catherine was a famous Russian monarch in European history, and she authored a "History of Russia". The British literary figure and idealist H.G. Wells caused a sensation in Europe and America with his "Outline of History", which has also been translated in our country. Wells' ideal work, "The Shape of Things to Come", has been acquired by a London film company for adaptation into a film. Wells pays close attention to the film industry and has recently been visiting various British film companies. The figure (A) shows him visiting the set while Douglas Fairbanks, Jr. is filming. The second person from the right is Wells, and the last person on the left is director Paul Czinner.

Regarding America: The German Emil Ludwig, famous for his biographies of historical figures such as "Napoleon", "Bismarck", "Goethe", and "Lincoln", recently had his masterpiece "Napoleon" acquired for filming by MGM, who hired him as a consultant for the film. Although Ludwig is a world-renowned biographer, he is very interested in film and has met many film industry figures during his visit to Hollywood, among whom Charlie Chaplin is the most highly regarded. He says that Chaplin's life story is enough material for him to write a biography, but he believes that Chaplin's personality is extremely complex, and he needs sufficient time to fully understand his dynamic character. Finally, Ludwig visited United Artists, the company to which Chaplin belongs, and happened to meet the comedic star Eddie Cantor and a group of United Artists executives. The figure (B) shows the scene taken at the United Artists studio, with the person standing to Ludwig's right being Darryl F. Zanuck, the producer of "42nd Street" and "Gold Diggers" from Warner Bros.

Film Reviews

Review of "Bombshell"

— Ling He

When film artists lack good material, they depict their own lives. This may be because the general public is very envious of the private lives of stars, so these sketches of star private lives have become fragrant bait for fishing. The audience's foreign coins and banknotes fill the pockets of the producers.

On the other hand, film artists using their own lives as the object of depiction is like novelists writing novels centered on novelists. It will certainly be more authentic because it is depicting oneself. As for film entrepreneurs selling the secrets of the studio, it is ultimately a

pathetic and laughable method of last resort.

"Bombshell", like last year's "Hollywood on Parade", is a record of the lives of stars. As mentioned above, this kind of record is indeed written very authentically.

An actress becomes a famous star due to the promotion of the company's publicity manager. As a result, her life becomes luxurious and comfortable. Many men pursue her. Her every move becomes the best material for newspapers. At this time, she does not refuse to associate with the person who promotes her and must also deal with the director. At the same time, because of the rascality of her father and brother, she tries to cover up all the ugly things. Like old-fashioned parents who do not want their sons to marry ugly female stars, so-called true love seems to have nothing to do with them.

These should be true depictions of their private lives. However, the screenwriter cleverly wrote the publicity manager, played by Lee Tracy, as a master of seduction, and said that the reason why noble sons cannot marry female stars is entirely due to his cunning manipulation, as if to explain that there is nothing between them. In fact, we feel that it is unnecessary. Anyway, the ugly society teaches people to live in ugliness. Everything is not a superficial moral issue that can explain all social phenomena, are our subjects, but when we choose subjects, we must strictly use good subjects. We certainly do not agree with the author using the method of makeup to cover up the truth, and they even intersperse this subject into a light and boring story of seduction, which is even more unacceptable to us. However, here, we can see the American casual and happy style.

In terms of being carefree and happy, not only are Lee Tracy and Jean Harlow the most suitable actors, but the director is also a master of this. He writes Jean Harlow as a typical American movie star, not only starting from powdering and applying lipstick, but also depicting the scene where a maid leads three dogs entangled around her, which is even more profound and detailed. As for Lee Tracy, with his eloquent specialty, playing a clever, lively, and brazen role, he also has special success. Since films such as "Moscow Nights" and "The Mayor of Hell", his nonsense skills will not be forgotten. In addition, Frank Morgan also performed very well.

As for the expensive sets and clear sound, they are originally the characteristics of American films. People who intend to be entertained may as well have a happy time.

Gary Cooper Loses and Regains Love

— Xi Lin

Yesterday, I saw Mr. Donglin's "Gary Cooper's Broken Heart" news in the Shen Bao Film Supplement. I felt that the text was a bit of a hindsight, because while he was talking about Gary Cooper's broken heart, Gary Cooper had already found his lover and was already engaged to her. That lucky woman is called Sandra Shaw. She was originally a famous New York socialite, originally named Veronica Balfe. She has an uncle named Cedric Gibbons, who is a producer in Hollywood, and his wife is Dolores del Río, the star of "Bird of Paradise". A year ago, Sandra came to Hollywood to visit her uncle, and Dolores held a grand banquet for her to entertain guests. Many producers saw her at the banquet and were amazed by her beauty, and they all asked her to act in movies. She first signed a six-month contract with RKO, and later transferred to Goldwyn. Although she is a newcomer to the film industry and lacks experience, she cannot play major roles, but her bright future is guaranteed by everyone. Unexpectedly, she later met Gary Cooper and fell in love at first sight, willing to give up her career as a star and marry a film person. Not long ago, she had already agreed with Gary Cooper to return to New York to meet her future parents-in-law, and it is expected that they will soon become a loving couple.

Furthermore, Gary Cooper's parents were extremely opposed to all his previous romances, such as with Clara Bow and Lupe Vélez, etc., but now they are very much in favor of this Sandra Shaw, and they say that Miss Shaw will definitely be a good wife and mother in the future, so the two elders are very happy to have a good son and daughter-in-law.

Family Harmony Also Needs to be Declared in the Newspaper

— Fu

It is common to publish marriage announcements in the newspaper, and it is also common to publish divorce announcements. But it is strange to publish something in the newspaper that is neither a marriage nor a divorce. Recently, Hollywood stars Neil Hamilton and his wife, because of rumors that they would soon divorce, posted an announcement in a newspaper saying: "Mr. and Mrs. Neil Hamilton hereby solemnly declare that they

have been married for eleven years, and their relationship has always been very deep. Although there have been various rumors in the outside world, which have been published in this newspaper and all other newspapers, and there have been various hearsay rumors: slander and gossip, which are quite terrible. We hereby inform the public that the past eleven years have been harmonious and seamless: and countless eleven years to come will continue in the same way, without change," etc. From the above advertisement, it can also be seen that Hollywood is shaken by the divorce trend, so that the families of ordinary people are shaken by it.

Film Novel

Broadway Thru a Keyhole (6)

— Xin Zhi

Clark asked her to dance, and she was even more flattered and flustered. She spun on the smooth floor to the soft music of the foxtrot; she wanted to close her eyes and have an endless beautiful dream, she was running in the clouds illuminated by the moonlight, she was relying on only a handsome man's arms, embracing her waist very securely. Soon, the night came to an end, and Clark came to see her again the next day, and came to see her every day. They swam together by the sea, galloped together in the wilderness, and lay drunk and dreamy in the cool shade of the palm trees. When the sun and moon were dim and only the stars were shining in the sky, they were still wandering on the beach. It was on such a night that Clark first pulled Joan Holland into his arms, and for the first time his lips met hers. When he hugged her tightly, she did not resist at all, and she simply closed her eyes and enjoyed the unrestrained, passionate kiss of the person she had long loved.

It was late at night when she hurriedly returned to the hotel. In the hallway of the hotel, there happened to be a member of Locky's gang, whom Joan originally knew, but because Joan arrogantly ignored him, he held a grudge and immediately sent a telegram to Chuck, telling him to report all of Joan Holland's actions to Locky. Five minutes later, Locky made a long-distance call, ordering Joan Holland to return to New York immediately. Joan returned to New York, where Locky and Chuck greeted her at the station and immediately took her to her apartment. When Joan arrived at the apartment, she took off her coat, and Locky immediately questioned her about the affairs in Erie. Joan initially wanted to hide it, but then Locky said Clark Brian's name and asked what was going on. He said, "It's not that I don't trust you, but I must know my own position. I have always taken care of you first, and you know it yourself. You say that I treat you so well, that's all my own willingness, there's no need to mention it. You don't owe me anything either. Just knowing you is already my reward. But if you want any changes, why not tell us and we can discuss it." Joan was afraid that something would be unfavorable to Clark, and in the end, she did not dare to tell him the truth, only saying, "Don't you know my heart?" Locky then picked her up and kissed her passionately. On the one hand, she did not dare to disobey Locky, and on the other hand, she felt sorry for Clark.

Soon after Joan Holland returned to New York, she saw a small news item in the newspaper saying that Clark Brian had been sued by the manager of a dance hall in Erie for breaking the contract and demanded compensation of $100,000. When she saw this news, she felt as if a great disaster was coming and became uneasy. One night, after her performance, she was about to remove her makeup in the dressing room when suddenly there was a knock on the door. She thought it was Locky, so she shouted, "Come in." But the person she saw coming in the mirror was not Locky, but Clark Brian. She floated around and was hugged by Clark. For a moment, she forgot everything, only Clark's fiery hot kiss. She whispered, "Oh, Clark, I missed you so much. Hold me tighter so I can feel that you really came. I will never let you leave me again." After Clark hugged her tightly, she suddenly shivered and quickly pushed him away, staring at him and saying, "How did you come? What if Locky finds out?" (To be continued)
